Methyl-P-Hydroxybenzoate  2.0 2.0 10.2 10.0 5.0 5.5 0.1 0.2 5.0 0.3 59.7  9. Sorbitol (70%) 10.Borax 1 1 .Water Procedure: Weigh 1-5 and heat to 85C with slow agitation. This wax blend has a cloud point o f 79C. Above the cloud point all waxes will eventually dissolve in blend. I f a higher solvating temperature is used, solvation can be much faster. Hold the wax blend at 70-8OC and add 6 and 7 to it with stirring until all has dissolved. Heat 8-11 to 85-9OC and stir gently until all has dissolved. Hold at 70-8OC. Place wax blend i n mixing container, add aqueous phase to it and shear with homomixer or colloid mill. At 53C the crude dispersion inverts and a thick creamy emulsion forms. Continue shearing while scraping the sides of the container to make sure the whole content is properly sheared. Add perfume, de-aerate and package.
